Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient; et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the way to treat it is for the patient to lie on his back, then the tip and shaft of the penis are made as hard as a feather, with the opening in the middle, as it should be; and beware of bleeding that often occurs, and if it does, stanch it with what stanches blood, and cure the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	of pimples on the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide; et en i a malignes et non malignes; si covient que tu les preignes a .i. oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien; puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	Many times this albata occurs in the penis, and it is an ugly-looking swelling; there are both malignant and non-malignant ones; you should grab them with a pair of tweezers, pull them out carefully, then clean and dry them thoroughly, apply moistened cotton wool in Egyptian ointment, then treat the area with diaphenicon ointment until it heals.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the ulcer is malignant, of pus color and foul-smelling, then you must apply cautery.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier; et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	When you have cut it, and if the ulcer is on the shaft of the penis, and part of it is inside the skin and part outside, then you must first remove the ulcer that is inside; and when it is healed, treat the one outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion; si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Because when you treat it together, if the foreskin is not secured so that it is not pierced, and blackness and corruption come to the foreskin and the testicles; then all that is black and corrupt must be cut away, then apply the ointment of honey and flour made from pomegranate bark and vetches, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if there is bleeding, bring the lunar cautery according to this form:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble: c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption; et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi; et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars; et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil; puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	The cauteries help in two ways together: that is, for bleeding and corruption; and if the foreskin is infected and retracted, you must insert a tube into the urethra and let the patient urinate through it; and when the foreskin is sore at the tip of the penis, which happens to those who have not been circumcised, or due to a wound or an abscess, then you must cut it with an instrument made of lead, until the foreskin is separated from the glans and is completely freed from the penis; and if it is a serious matter to discuss this, then you should cut it with a spatula made of some soft metal at the tip of the penis and the skin; then separate them gently, and place a thin linen cloth wet in cold water between them so that it does not become sore again.
de la circoncision	of circumcision
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies; toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	Circumcision is not like other wounds in terms of healing; however, when we perform this procedure intentionally, especially on infants, it is necessary to do it properly and gently for their well-being.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancient authors did not describe the circumcision of their children because they did not practice it in their law, and we only have what we have acquired through experimentation.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor .i. dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule; si fuioit li keurs car il i a .ij. toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	Because I have seen most of the masters and surgeons who performed circumcision all around the glans, and in some cases even cut off the foreskin entirely; this caused the skin to dry out and form a scar, as there were two membranes, and sometimes the upper one was removed while the lower one remained.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre; et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	Then they cover it again, and the pain is doubled, and with the washing of the glans, which is not healed at the tip of the member; and in washing the nail, sometimes the instrument slips, and they injure the work, and many times they grow back so that they don't need to be washed, and I have seen this.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the washing that is done around the glans, I have found the goodness of the experiment, for the forces cut accurately both above and below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens; mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir; et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues; puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens; puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens; puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien; et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge; puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres; et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Because when you press your hand, you cut it evenly into the entire soul; but let the thread be tightly wound around the skin; and the manner of the first work is that you make the child think, if he understands, that you are only tying the thread around the wand, and then you make him stretch in all the ways you can; then make him stand between your hands straight up, and support his weight with your hands or under your feet so that the child does not see them, or any of the instruments; then place your hand on the wand and breathe into the heart, and draw it upwards until the head of the wand is inside; then cleanse it well of the dirt that has accumulated there, then tie the place marked with a double thread, then tie it under the other end; hold it with both hands by the second bond at the pouch and the index finger, and press between the two bonds, then lift the heart quickly and draw the head of the wand; then let the blood flow little by little, for that is the wound; and put powder on top of the powder, a cloth glued with an egg cooked in rose water, confit with good and fresh rosemary oil, and leave it until the next day, and cure it again and again until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste: li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	The shape of the forceps for cleansing should be as follows: the two heads should be thin and sharp, and the handles should be as wide as the palm of the hand equally.
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision; donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme; et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	The mistake in cleansing is when the glans slips inside during incising; therefore, you must stretch it with your nail so that the glans makes an abscess; then, press equally and if you cannot hold it with your nail, hold it with tweezers, then press.
Et s’il trespassent .iij. jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement; si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	And if it persists for 3 days, and that which is under the foreskin is swollen, let it be until the hot abscess is soothed and the skin is lightly scratched; then copulate as much as you can, being careful not to touch the foreskin, this will do him no harm.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point; cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Treat therefore the area of sudden wounds with powder, as we have said in the treatise on powders, and if he copulates beyond measure, and it goes above, it will do no harm; treat it therefore, as we have said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	from the retention of urine
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division; et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz; et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet; et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e; et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme: et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil; et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	The retention of urine is due to a stone, or congelated blood, or a tumor, or similar conditions that we have described in the division; and if the urine is not released, and you see that the retention is caused by the stone lodged at the neck of the bladder, then the patient should be bent forward at the waist, with his feet placed on his back, and his abdomen pressed down from above the back, and he should strain as hard as he can; thus the neck of the bladder will be forced upward to expel the stone, and the urine will be released. If it does not come out as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must administer an extraction using a syringe, which is called a "syringe". It should be made of thin silver like a bird's feather; its tube should be a palm and a half long, and thin at the tip.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue; et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede; puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude; puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors; puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine; et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	And the way of the issue of urine is that you take a double thread and tie it to the head with a little wool or cotton, and insert the end of the thread into the syringe; then squeeze out the excess wool and fill the syringe to the top, then anoint the syringe with oil or butter and egg white; have the patient sit on a chair, and lubricate the bladder and penis with moist oil, olive oil, and warm water; then gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches the root of the penis, then double the penis over towards the scrotum; next, fill the syringe all the way to the bladder, and feel the patient urinate until the bladder is empty; if this is not done in this order, but according to another method, then the person guiding the stream is wrong; then pull out the thread through the wool, and let the urine run through the wool; then remove it, and pass the urine; then reinsert the syringe until the bladder is emptied and the patient is relieved.
des maladies de la vessie	of diseases of the bladder
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When scabs or blood come in the bladder, or pus is accumulated there, and you see water and medicine dripping from it, then do this with all the apparatus that is called a "clepsydra", and this is how:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus: II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois; et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est; et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens; si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens; si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira; et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie: si est ci:	It is closed and has three openings: two on one side and one on the other, as you can see; and the medicine-carrying tube through which the medicine is applied should be such that it blocks the urethra without addition, so that if moisture can be extracted, and pushed when necessary; and when you see your medicines moving in the bladder, put the tip of the catheter into the moisture and draw it along, so that the moisture will enter the catheter and then return to the bladder, so that the patient feels it; and this is the form of the subtle catheter by which one catheters the bladder: thus it is:
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut; et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet; puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu; puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie; et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor; puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument; et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And it is made of silver or bronze, and the tip is higher up; and underneath there is a testicle or a scrotum; then take a sheep's bladder and put in it the moisture by which you want to catheterize the bladder, then tie it between the two testicles with a strong double thread, and heat this moisture over the fire; then insert the tip of the catheter into the urethra, then apply your hand to the bladder to draw all the moisture in smoothly, so that the patient feels that this moisture has reached the bladder; and if you do not have a bladder, take a piece of parchment and make it into a circle, and pierce it all around; then insert the thread tightly through these openings, then assemble the circle as one assembles a shield, and put inside what you want of oil and moisture and water, and attach it to the instrument; and do as you did with the bladder, by squeezing with your hand until the moisture reaches the bladder.
de la piere	of stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines; et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille; et en la vessie, et en la verge; et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	We have already discussed in the division the ways of stone, and its extraction along with medicines; and I have described the difference between a stone lodged in the bladder, and all the signs, and in which type of stone one should operate: in the bladder, and in the penis; and I will tell you plainly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit; et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist; et a mout de ces saut li fondemens; et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont .iiij. ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece; et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	I say that the stone which is lodged in the bladder occurs most often in children, and it is a sign that the water flows from the bladder, resembling water in its subtlety; and it causes pain to the patient, and he grasps his penis, and can urinate many times, and then it blocks; and many of these cause the foundation [of the body]; and healing is easier for children until they are 4 years old, and it is much more serious in the elderly, and it is midway between youth and old age; and the cure is generally easier for those who have larger stones than for those with smaller ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is necessary first to cleanse the patient with an enema, to draw out all the feces that are in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For it sometimes clogs up while seeking the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut; puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval; puis la quier et la touche dedens; se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	Then take the patient by the feet and make him stand up and move around so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it comes out from the top; then have him sit between your hands, with his hands under his thighs, so that the bladder is completely tilted downward; then examine and feel inside; if you feel the stone in the passage, hurry now to cut on the stone.
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis; et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie; puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	And if it does not come out with just the touch, then wet your index finger of the left hand with oil, if the patient is an adult, or with your middle finger if the patient is a young person; and insert it into his anus, and examine for the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, pull it toward the neck of the bladder; then press against it with your finger, and move it away from where you intend to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille; puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	And instruct the minister to press on the bladder with his hand, and tell him to lift up the testicles with his right hand, and with his left hand pull back the skin underneath the testicles in the area where the incision is made; then insert the spatulum firmly, following its natural curve.Et s’il sent la piere a son doi indice ou moien, si quier la piere avec li spatumile et li boutons dedens, et quant il la sens, si l’amoine vers le col de la vessie;
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre; et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans; par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail; et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges: si est griés a issir; et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	And they cut between what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the side of the left buttock; and it should be straight over the stone, and both hands should be pressed against the anus, and the incision should be made across the navel so that it is wide on top and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large; perhaps it presses on the hand which is against the anus, so that it pops out without any effort. And you will find that there is a kind of stone with angles and edges, which is hard to remove; and there is another type which is underneath, resembling a gland, and round, whose extraction is easier.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant; et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe; ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief; et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole; et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	And for those with angles and edges, make the incision larger; and if it does not come out, then you must grip it with forceps which are like a file at the tip, to pull out the stone so that it does not slip away; or you push underneath with a thin instrument curved at the end; and if you cannot grab it thus, then widen the opening and pour vinegar inside, and if there is more than one stone, first insert the largest one into the neck of the bladder, then press in from above, then pull it out, and the smaller ones afterwards if there are several.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, it must be sutured, and a larger wound made.
Car II choses avienent au malaide: ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder; mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces; et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut; puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	For two things happen to the patient: either he dies or his urine comes out through the place where the urethra cannot heal; but nevertheless, try to pull it out with tweezers until you have extracted it in pieces; and when you have finished your work, smear the wound with incense and aloe and dragon's blood, and compress it, and place a damp cloth soaked in oil and wine, or oil and rosewater and cold water, over the abscess to soothe the hot swelling; then re-insert the catheter into his penis, and do not remove the ligature until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you loosen it, then wash the site well with oil and water, then treat the wound with thin ointment and thick ointment until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine: boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit; puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez; et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And if hot abscesses and corrosions of blood come into the wound and the bladder is blocked by this so that urine cannot pass through it in a healthy manner: then press your finger into the wound and extract that blood, for if it remains there, it will corrupt the bladder and cause it to protrude; then wash the wound with water and vinegar and celery seed, and treat him in all the ways you know until he is healed; and it is necessary that every day that you dress his wound, you bind his two thighs together, and assemble the remedies over the affected area.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir; si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	And if the stone is small and it is in the urethra, and lodged in it, so that urine cannot pass; then the treatment of what I have said before serves as an excuse for cutting many times.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have experienced this myself.
Pren .i. foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a .iij. angles fichiees en .i. tison:	Take an iron rod according to this form and let it be filed into three angles:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie; puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere; et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part; si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	Then take a thread and tie it around the penis under the stone, so that it cannot go back into the bladder; then push the needle into the penis gently, until it reaches the stone; then turn the needle in your hand within the stone little by little, until you can pierce the stone from another side; then urine will flow at once, then press your hand on what remains of the stone that is inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides; et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If it is broken at once and comes out with the urine, then the patient is cured; and if you cannot do this for any reason that causes it to come out, then tie a thread under the stone and another above it, then cut into the penis towards the stone between the two threads, then pull it out, and untie the thread, and cleanse the congealed blood that is in the wound; and treat it until it is healed.
de la piere des femmes	of the stones of women
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por .iij. choses: l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge; et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	Sometimes stones form in women, and if they do, the cure is difficult, and it is prohibited for three reasons: one is that perhaps the woman is a virgin; and the second is that one cannot find a skilled woman who reveals herself to midwives, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains; et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil; et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere; et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge: adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere; et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	And the third way is that by chance one cannot find a woman well skilled in this art of medicine; and the fourth way is that the woman's stone is more deeply embedded than a man's, so it requires a deeper incision, and there is great fear involved. And if necessity demands it, then you should take a midwife who is well skilled, and with difficulty pierce her, and if you cannot pierce her, then do not want to use a very subtle needle; and present her with a cupping glass that is well-made for the treatment of women, or a woman who knows part of the art, and command her to do what you command in the examination of the stone; and look very carefully to see if the woman is a virgin. Then she should insert her finger into the opening and search for the stone; and if she finds it, then hold it under her finger, and recommend that she inserts her finger where the pain is located, and press her left hand firmly on the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse; puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie; et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite; puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont: c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	If she has a hernia, she should move it gradually from the entrance of the bladder down to the root of the thigh; then press on the stone at the root of the thigh against the middle of the groin, where the stone is located and feels tender; do not move your finger above or below the stone, and make the incision small at first. Then open the wound as wide as you can sense the stone, so that it can come out; know that there are many types of stones: small ones, large ones, smooth ones, sharp ones, long ones, round ones, and those with rays.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	And if you know their appearances in order to identify the cause.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez; puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre; et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide; puis cure la plaie.	And if you feel any bleeding, put crushed vitriol over the spot and hold it there for an hour until the bleeding stops; then return to your work so that the stone can come out, and have some of the instruments I told you about earlier for extracting stones from men to assist you in your task. If you feel bleeding, and it is from a cut artery, put the powder on the spot and constrict it with bandages and cloth; do not apply anything else, leave the stone alone, and do not try to pull it out or the patient may die; then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood has subsided and the site has healed, return to your work until the stone is removed.
de hernie carnouse	of carnous hernia
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef; et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit .i. autre oef; et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit; et ceu n’avient se poc non.	Aquous fluid is nothing else but an assembly of moisture or white pus, which is beneath the heart of the testicles, containing the egg; and is called "pus", and sometimes it is properly in the membrane of the egg, if one thinks that it is another egg; and that is the skin of the testicle between the white pus that we have mentioned. And this does not happen rarely.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this disease is due to weakness that comes to the testicles, and that matter is spread out.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors: ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus; et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	And sometimes it comes from a blow to the testicles, and this moisture has many colors; sometimes it is a yellow complexion, sometimes red-less, sometimes black, sometimes watery white, and so on; and these are the signs by which we know this condition, for if it is in the white syphilis that we have described, then the abscesses are ready, small like the shape of an egg, and they do not appear on the testicles because there is moisture all around them.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef; et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien; donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	And if there is moisture in the skin itself, then the abscesses are ready with part of an egg, and so one thinks it is another egg; and if the moisture is between the skin of the testicles and the white syphilis, then he feels good; therefore, when you want to know the color of the moisture, test all over the scrotum, for its shape is as described above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to this then, what comes after the entrance, judge what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors; puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz; puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions; puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir; puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont; et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement; cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue; et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac; puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when we treat it with iron, the patient should be healed according to his strength and the fullness of his body; then he lies on his back on something slightly raised, and many layers of cloth are placed under him; then he sits up, and the assistant sits opposite on the right, and the rod is extended to one of the two ribs below the heart; then take the spatulum and gently lift the skin of the ribs from their tips all the way to the armpit, and the split should be straight as you lift the ribcage skin up to the white part of the shoulder blade, and scrape gently according to your strength; then pierce the shoulder blade with a large hole, and draw out all the water, and then put in your fingers, and press the shoulder blade upwards; and do not touch the ribs, only the shoulder blade; gently lift the ribcage all around just as much as you can, for if you do not lift it well, the water will return; and if an egg is damaged in your work, return it to its place when you have finished the work on the shoulder blade; then sew the two edges of the ribs together with one stitch, then cure it like other wounds until it heals.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc; puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	And if you find that the testicle is corrupted by another disease, then you must ligate the vessels which are suspended, fearing a rupture of blood; then cut the scrotum all around the suspension, extract the testicle and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices; si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset; et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	And if the water is collected in two parts together, know that they are two blisters; then cup the other part as you did the first, equally, then wipe away the blood and put on the wound soft lamb's wool moistened with rose oil; and moisten another piece of lamb's wool with wine and oil, and place it over both blisters, and place doubled linen over them, and bind it firmly all around according to this form.
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil; et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier; et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers; si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Then take two pieces of linen and stuff them with lamb's wool according to this pattern, and sew them together at the crotch of the breeches, and let one piece hang over the anus onto the back, and the other onto the perineum; and let both ends hang over the two angles, and tie all around the buckle of the breeches firmly. Sometimes this blister is treated with a cautery instead of cutting with iron, and it is done by grasping a small, thin cautery knife, and scorching the skin of the blisters, so that the white pus contained in the water is exposed; then take the cautery according to this form, and pierce that pus at the edges, and scorch it with this thin hot cautery.
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout; et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef; et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve; et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille; et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	And the cup in every way that you can, as long as you stretch everything out; and be careful not to let the fire touch the egg; and know that this work is safer; and move carefully to avoid blood flow, and changes that affect the wound; and if anything contradicts this, whether it is an abscess or blood flow or anything else, then cure what contradicts it according to what has been said before.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit; pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors; et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer; puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee; et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant; et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	And if the patient is fearful and does not want to undergo this treatment due to its horribleness, then prepare for incision as I have told you; it is necessary for the patient to sit on a raised seat; then pierce the abscess in the lower part, throughout the spatulum, and insert the incision deeply into the body; make the holes wide so that all the pus can flow out; then place cotton over the area, and bandage it, and let the remaining pus drain out, and then cure the wound until it is healed; and if the white membrane does not allow the pus to flow out through the mouth of the wound, then you must insert a feather or the instrument used to treat hydrops, of which the shape has been described earlier; widen the wound, and know that the pus will return, and be re-absorbed after six months or so, and when it is re-absorbed as before, and thus the patient's condition will improve over time.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles:
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse; et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	Know that in the dissection of this armpit there are many dispositions of fear, because of which I think it is better to leave it alone. And I will tell you the operation and the appearances of the abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions; et c’est par mout de cas.	I therefore say that many abscesses come in the body, especially in the testicles; and this happens in many cases.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion; et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors; et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief; et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	This is to be known through an abundance of bitterness and ague, which is spread throughout the body, or from a blow; and the color of the abscess follows the color of the body; and it does not subside in pain, and it is a grave abscess; and sometimes there are dark, fearful, and piercing abscesses, and a flowing color, and at times it comes from a rupture of an artery, or from inflammation of a vein.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois; et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	When it is from a rupture of an artery, it is known by the warm disposition of the abscess, when you press it with your fingers; and you must not touch it.Quant c’est par enfleure de voine, il est conus par la coler del aposteme; et li color vairent, si com il vait a la coler del corps; et covient que tu le mettes a tuit repos et a tuit grant calm; et ne covient mie que tu le fesses bouillir, ne l’enleves en aucun manier.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars; et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	Those who are affected by inflammation of the vein are known by their appearance and the sensation when touched with the fingers; anyone can then make a diagnosis based on this examination and similar examinations of other parts of the body. You should examine the color of the eyelids, then lift the eyelid to expose the eyeball, and note any white film over the eyeball.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope; et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	If the eyeball is already affected by these symptoms, then you must treat the eyeball and the eyelid; if there is a film over the eyeball or within the blood vessels, then you must remove all of that film and smooth out the surface.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the growth is in the back, then you must cut it all out and extract the egg, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when your work is finished, then dress the wound with wool moistened in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	of the abscess of the testicles:
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait; et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	This is an abscess wrapped in a swelling that resembles a grape, with the softening of the eyelids, and when the patient blinks, it causes great pain; the treatment for this condition is very similar to the previous one, and although we will describe its procedure according to the methods of the ancients, it is a very dangerous treatment.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment; puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples; puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief; puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues; puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions; car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz; si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	It is necessary for you to make the patient sit on an elevated seat, then tie the suspensory of the testicles down with your fingers, pressing all the vessels that are near the penis, and tighten them, then cut through the vessels with a sharp knife, widely and directly, until they are exposed, and then scrape from each side, as we have said in the extraction of the arteries in the temples; then insert a needle where there is a double thread, and tie it to the first place where the vein appeared, and tie it directly to the other end; then pull them gently, following the length of the body, and draw out the corrupted moisture; then cure the wound as with the others, or insert a bowstring, so that any vessel that is cut off from the testicles does not lose its nourishment due to the cutting of the vessels, and dry up and cannot heal.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rot of the eye socket
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions; et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes: ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses; et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement; et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	The occurrences of this hernia are through the incision that comes from the scrotum, or the extension over the abdomen in the region of the inguinal canal, causing the intestines to descend from that passage to one of the groins; and this passage is at the level of the scrotum, or from its extension, and these two types of hernia come from many causes: from a blow, or jumping, or coughing, or lifting a heavy load, and similar activities. The signs when it is from an extension of the scrotum are that it happens gradually over a long time, and does not come on suddenly; and the hernias are equal in size up to the depth, because the scrotum presses on the intestines.
Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the sign is when it is from dysentery, that it causes sudden pain at the beginning, and the abscesses are various appearances below the skin, and it is due to the exit of the intestine and the body's defense against dysentery.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the peritonitis is retained inside, and it causes great suffering to the patient, especially when it is pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these cures of iron there is fear, which is why one should avoid it.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir; puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes; puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc; puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir; puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars; puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac; et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille; et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement; et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz; puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions; aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz; puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars; puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne; et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi; et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte; puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant; puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	And the method of treatment is to instruct the patient to push the intestine back into the wound with his hand if he can; then hold the scrotum between your hands and lift the buttocks; then press the abdomen down, and grab all the skin of the groin from the top; then insert the hooks of the retractor into the incision according to what you need in order to open the wound, and make it so that the aorta can come out; then scrape off the scrotum under the skin of the testicles, until the tough white scrotum is exposed all around; then put your index finger into the scrotum behind one of the testicles, into what is between the white scrotum under the skin of the testicle and between the second scrotum, and separate what is behind the testicle and between the second scrotum; then move your right hand inside the scrotum, and hold the white scrotum up in your left hand, and lift the testicle with all the scrotum towards the abdomen; and instruct an assistant to stretch the testicle upwards, and untie what is behind the bandage; then feel with your fingers if there is any intestine wrapped around the tough white scrotum, and if you find anything, pull it back into the abdomen; then take a needle with a thick thread made from ten fibers, and insert it into the back part of the scrotum, which is behind the skin of the testicles; after the incision, grab the parts of the threads, so that there are four threads; then tie them together in a cross shape, and tie the scrotum with a strong ligature in two places; then wrap the thread around the scrotum tightly, so that none of the blood vessels that nourish it can pass through, so that no hernia occurs; then put the ligature according to the first long ligature two fingers from that one, and after these two ligatures leave a space of a finger's width in the scrotum behind the testicle; then grab the part under the skin of the scrotum, as we said before, so that the blood flows, and treat the wound with soft wool soaked in oil; then put on the ligature as we said.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes the white syphilitic sore which we have described is cauterized after an incision out of fear of bleeding.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui; et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece; puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	For this often happens, and let the wound bleed as much as it can; and if it is slow to heal, then use hot water, and apply what we have said until it heals; then cure the wound with another cure, until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	of carnous hernia
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this remedy I have never seen anyone dare to perform the cure with iron.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz; puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient; et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And the ancients say that it is done like the ramie which is tied together with the vis, in such a way that you tie the vessels, after cutting above gently to the bottom; then coppice with myrrh, and cure the abscess with what works, until the vessels heal; and cure it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus; et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres; et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent; et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert; et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit; et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere: et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois; et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac; et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre; puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines; puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	Sometimes the rut comes out in the veins, as we have said, and opens the place; and no intestines come out into the bowels, and if any do, it is a little, and repair every hour; and nevertheless if he stays too long in this state, he believes the wound or the fistula, so that the intestines come out; and this happens because of the extension of the fistula which is in the veins, as we have said, for it extends, then becomes soft and swollen at the place and opens; and its cure is by cautery, as we have previously said; and sometimes it is cured by iron in this way: and the patient lies down on his back between your hands, then coppice the rut that is swollen with salt according to the quantity of three eggs; and then draw out the fistula which is under the skin, then take the thread and place it over the apparent place of the fistula; and press it deeply into the abdomen, then cut the two apparent places of the fistula on the top of the thread, and cut one and the other; then pull out the top of the thread, and do not cover the fistula or extend the egg or anything else, as I have made you aware in the cure of a rupture of the intestines; then cure it by the cure of wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the threads, cleanse and treat the wound until it heals.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The ulcer is constrained, and has no appearance in the wound, and cautery is effective in this case, and closer to safety.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of the softening of the skin of the scrotum
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir; et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil; puis assemble les .ij. levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a .iij. costures ou .iiij. fermement; puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Many times the skin of the scrotum softens in some men due to the testicles within becoming softened, and it is milky in appearance; and when one wishes to treat it, they should make the patient lie on his back, and cut the softened skin on the skin of the scrotum; then bring together the two edges with a single stitch, or at most two or three stitches, firmly; then cut between the stitches, and treat it as you would other wounds, until it is healed, and remove the sutures.
dou chastrement	of chastisement
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre; et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres: dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure; et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	You should know that castration is condemned by our law, and for this reason I would prefer not to discuss it in this book. However, there are two reasons why knowledge of it is necessary: the first is so that the doctor can answer questions about it and know how to perform the procedure; the second is because we often need to castrate certain animals to help us, such as bulls, rams, horses, and other beasts.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres: ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	I say therefore that castration is done in two ways: either by attraction or by cutting.Atraction se fait a l’aide d’un fer chaud et d’un cautere; la fendure, en coupant avec un couteau.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant; puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	In that which we do by attraction, we make the animal sit in hot water so that its testicles are softened and hanging down; then squeeze them with your hand until they are put back into place and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille: covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez; et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz; et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure; puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	On castration: you must tie the animal down, and press the scrotum with your left hand, then tie the suspenders, and cut on each testicle, once you have cut them well; and leave some pus of the syphilis and the subtle syphilis which is over the vessels; and this method of castration is better than that done by attraction, because with attraction something of the testicles might remain, causing the animal to desire lust; then treat the wound until it heals.
des hermofrodites	of hermaphrodites
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes: l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	Hermaphroditism occurs in two ways in males: one is that between the testicles there appears something like the form of nature of a woman, and it has hair, and sometimes urates.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And the other manner is in women, and has above the wrist as a rod and two testicles.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies; en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	And the treatment of men and women is to cut off the scrotum, and treat it like any other wound; in the second manner, for men whose semen leaks through the skin of the testicles, there is no cure.
de la tentigene	of the tentigenes
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir; et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	A hernia is an external swelling above the natural part, so large that it is ugly to look at; and some women have them as large as a hand, and that is the cure.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement; et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	You should dye the excess of the hernia with your hand or a knife, and cut it slightly; and do not cut too deep so that bleeding does not occur, then treat one wound with another cure until it is healed; and for a swelling that occurs in the mouth of the vagina, use it, and perhaps it will burst, and it is like the appearance of a cow, and because of this the ancients called it the "cow disease.
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	If you need to treat it, as we have said before, treat the wound until it is healed.
de erratique	of erratics
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis; et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est; ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit; et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir; et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	It is erratic when the nature of the woman is not understood, or the passage is small; and it is natural by birth, or accidental due to illness that comes to it; or it is caused by a foreign object, or a sottish or thick suppuration, and is formed deep in the body, or on the sides, or underneath, or wherever it may be; and they should understand conception and childbirth, and perhaps flowers to have; and the knowledge of this is through the observation of the dance.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the wound is nearby, appear with your fingers or on a rod.
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi: met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes; puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens; puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	If it is from a sottish suppuration and is nearby the lips, do this: place your two index fingers together, and let the woman lie on her back with her legs spread; then form the lips, so that the sottish suppuration is pierced, and cover the wound; then take wool, moisten it in oil, and place it on the spot, and let the woman lie at home every day so that it may not close up.Si la piere est en le costez de l’estomac, et li membres sont dislocuez:
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the syphilis is hard and thick, you must cut it with the spatula like a myrtle leaf.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope; et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef; puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder; et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec; puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the wound is of fresh flesh, then stop the bleeding and cut it; and have blood-stopping medicines like acacia, dragon's blood, incense, and egg white; then apply a wide bandage of loose linen so that the wound cannot heal; and let this be for a long time, and then apply a tent of dry linen; then treat with other treatments until it is healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when fresh flesh appears in a wound, it must be cut in this way, unless it is an abscess.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For one must not cut at an abscess that is within a wound.Et li apotemes qui sont en la marris ne doit on point coper selonc ceste maniere; mes covient les fendre si com dis, et li estrainer le pu pour que li sang ne fuie.
des emorroides	of hemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul; et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	Hemorrhoids are openings in veins from which blood flows habitually, and when hemorrhoids are old they become hard; and we have already said in the division their likenesses to hawks, and the signs, and I will now say those that receive a cure.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that hemorrhoids and hard hemorrhoids, when they are emp[er]f[ect] in the anus, and do not appear to the sense [of sight], except for the cure by iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those which are at the mouth of the anus, one can feel; they are those that can be cured.Li thelul et li emorroides qui sont desous la marris, il n’a pas de cure, si n’est par fer.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses; puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide; et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	One must then place the woman in a cold room, and heat the bed with tongs, and the pillow at its roots; then powder over restraining medicines such as acacia and dragon's blood and incense, and similar things; then bind her feet to the wall for an hour, then place her in cold water; and if bleeding ensues, have her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate rind and galls and similar things, and then take barley flour, and mix it with honey and garlic, and make a poultice over her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it stops, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir; puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	If not, have her breathe in steam from the back and breasts without burning; then take wool, and moisten it in plantain juice or dogwood juice mixed with old wine, and apply it to the area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul; et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the abscess has subsided, treat the area with ointment until it heals; and that which is called "albathir" is red, and resembles rough skin, so it should be covered as I have said with a bandage; and then treat it until it heals.
des apostemes de la marris	of absesses in the anus:
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	Many types of abscesses occur in the head, such as ulcers and pimple-like abscesses, and herpes, and estafettes, and fistulas, and hemorrhoids, and hot abscesses, and several other diseases which I have described in the divisions.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe; et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	Therefore, it is necessary that I describe in this treatise the hot abscess which occurs in the head; for there are many kinds of abscesses that burst in the bowels: and if you wish to know about iron treatment, observe whether the abscesses are hard at the beginning of their appearance, and filled with heat and fever, and whether they turn red when you look at them.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie; et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe; et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien; puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme; et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide; et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve; et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	Therefore, do not rush to pierce it, but let the pain subside first; then have the patient sit on a chair, and have two small seats for him to lean on, one on each side, and have him support his back and bend his legs to the sides; let his buttocks be spread apart, and have him place his arms under his knees, and tie them well with a good bandage. Then suck the wound towards the right rib, and administer the instrument used to open the wound, from which the pus will come out afterward; you must insert the rod first to determine the depth of the wound so that what goes into the wound does not go in too deep and cause bleeding or hurt the patient; if the instrument is larger, cover the depth of the wound with cloth so it does not irritate him. Have him hold the nozzle of the instrument above and breathe into the instrument.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit; et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec; et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites; puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez; et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites; puis reveigne a l’oignement.	And when the abscesses open, and they are made by the soft hand, then they should be covered with the head, or with the spatumile lead; and when the bowels are emptied, then you should put into the wound moist tents in rose oil, or in dry green oil; and place the tent outside the wound at the bottom of the injury, and place over the injury and over the small clean lamb's wool moistened in water or malva flowers that have been cooked; then heal after two days of ointment, until it is healed; and sometimes raise the injury and the wound by enema of water and honey, and then of water or roots of lilies and aristolochia that have been cooked for a long time; then return to the ointment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is pushed back into the injury, then you should be careful to cook with iron, but heal it as we have said in the division.
de l’enfantement	of childbirth
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar: adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir; adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui; et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost; car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification; et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	It is necessary first for the midwife to know the natural shape of childbirth, and the signs, which are when you see the woman push downward and desire to smell flowers; then the child rushes to be born; then you know that this childbirth follows nature's design, and the afterbirth comes out with the child, and the mother is cleansed of her excess fluids through proper cleansing; and those who come in a different way are not born naturally.
